GT Equivalence Verification (PO27)
============================================================
GT: F0*sin(t) - alpha*v**c0 - c1*beta*v - beta*exp(-Abs(v))*v
Candidate formulas: 60

GT (fixed):
\[
f(t,v)=0.66863216766915\sin t\;-\;0.0585985712804097\,v^3\;-\;0.716668620096812\,v\;-\;0.358334310048406\,v\,e^{-|v|}
\]
Key required structures:
- a pure sinusoid in \(t\) with **no amplitude dependence on \(v\)** (just \(A\sin t\));
- polynomial terms exactly \(v\) and \(v^3\);
- a damping term exactly \(v\exp(-|v|)\) (note the **minus** in the exponent and the **Abs**).

Trig note: any \(c\cos(t+\phi)\) can match \(A\sin t\) by choosing \(\phi=\pi/2\) (since \(\cos(t-\pi/2)=\sin t\)), and setting amplitude accordingly. Also \(\cos(c_2 t + c_3)\) can match \(\sin t\) only if \(c_2=1\) (or \(c_2=-1\) with phase adjustment).

Now check candidates.

1. \(c0 v + c1\cos(c2+t)+c3 v^3 + c4 v + c5 v e^{c6|v|}\)  
   Combine linear terms: \((c0+c4)v\) can match \(-0.7166v\). \(c3 v^3\) can match \(-0.0586v^3\). Cos term can match \(0.6686\sin t\) via phase shift. Exponential term: need \(-0.3583 v e^{-|v|}\) so set \(c6=-1\), \(c5=-0.3583\). Works. **Match possible.**

2. \(c0 v + c1 v^3 + c2\cos(c3+t)+c4 v e^{c5|v|}\)  
   Same as GT components; set \(c1=-0.058598...\), \(c0=-0.716668...\), \(c5=-1\), \(c4=-0.358334...\), and choose cosine phase/amplitude to equal \(0.668632\sin t\). **Match possible.**

3. \(c0 v + c1\cos(c2+t)+c3 v^{c4}+c5 v e^{c6|v|}\)  
   Can set \(c4=3\) and \(c3=-0.058598...\). Linear and exp and trig adjustable as above. **Match possible.**

4. Has \(v/(c4+|v|)\) term; GT has no such rational-in-\(|v|\) term. Only removable by setting its coefficient \(c3=0\). Then remaining terms can match as in (3) but note there is no explicit \(v^3\) unless created elsewhere—there isn’t. So cannot get \(v^3\) unless \(c5 v e^{c6|v|}\) somehow equals a cubic globally (impossible). **No match.**

5. Two terms \(v e^{c4|v|}\) and \(v e^{c6|v|}\); no polynomial \(v^3\). You could set one exp term to approximate polynomial locally but not equal for all \(v\). Setting one exp coefficient 0 still leaves no \(v^3\). **No match.**

6. Includes \(v|v|\) term; GT does not. Must set its coefficient \(c4=0\). Then it reduces to form like (2) with \(v, v^3, \cos, v e^{c6|v|}\) so can match by choosing \(c6=-1\) etc. **Match possible.**

7. Has \(v e^{c6 v^2}\) term; GT needs \(v e^{-|v|}\). No way to make \(e^{c6 v^2}=e^{-|v|}\) for all real \(v\). Also lacks explicit \(v^3\) unless via other terms (none). **No match.**

8. Has \(\cos(c2 t + c3)\) and \(v^{c5}\) and \(v e^{c7|v|}\). Set \(c2=1\) and phase to convert cosine to sine; set \(c5=3\) for cubic; set exp exponent coefficient \(c7=-1\). Also need linear \(v\) term: present as \(c0 v\). Works. **Match possible.**

9. \(c0 v + c1\cos(c2 t + c3)+c4 v e^{c5|v|}+c6 v^3\)  
   Directly matches with \(c2=1\), phase shift, \(c5=-1\), and coefficients set. **Match possible.**

10. Contains \(\sin(c5 v + c6)\), \(v|v|\), and \(v\log(\cdot)|v|\) terms; GT has none. You can zero those coefficients, but then you lose the needed \(v^3\) and \(v e^{-|v|}\) terms (not present). **No match.**

11. Has extra \(v e^{c6 x} e^{c7|v|}\) term depending on \(x\); GT has no \(x\)-dependence. Must set \(c5=0\) to remove it. Then remaining terms are \(v\), trig, and \(v e^{c4|v|}\) but no \(v^3\). **No match.**

12. Has constant and \(e^{c2 x}\) terms; must set \(c0=0\), \(c1=0\) to remove \(x\)-dependence/constant. Then has \(c3 v^{c4}+c5 v^3\): can set \(c4=1\) and use \(c3 v\) plus \(c5 v^3\). Trig term can match sine. Exp term can match with exponent \(-|v|\). Works. **Match possible.**

13. Has constant and \(e^{c2 x}\): set \(c0=0,c1=0\). Has two \(v^3\) terms \(c3 v^3+c4 v^3\) combine to needed cubic. Has linear \(c9 v\). Has \(v e^{c8|v|}\) and trig. Set \(c8=-1\). Works. **Match possible.**

14. Has constant and \(e^{c2 x}\): set \(c0=0,c1=0\). Remaining: \(c3 v^3 + c8 v + c6 v e^{c7|v|} + \cos\) which can match with \(c7=-1\) and phase shift. **Match possible.**

15. Has constant and \(c1 x\): GT has no constant or \(x\) term, so set \(c0=0,c1=0\). Then it’s \(c2 v + c3 v^3 + \cos + c6 v e^{c7|v|}\) which can match with \(c7=-1\) and phase shift. **Match possible.**

16. Has \(v|v|\) and \(v\log(\cdot)|v|\) terms; must set those coefficients to 0. Then left with \(c0 v + c1\cos(c2 t+c3)+c7 v^3\). Missing \(v e^{-|v|}\). **No match.**

17. Similar: even if set nonlinear abs/log terms to 0, no \(v e^{-|v|}\). **No match.**

18. Has \(v^{c5}\), \(v|v|\), and \(v\log(\cdot)|v|\) but no \(v e^{-|v|}\). Even if set abs/log terms to 0 and choose \(c5=3\), still missing exponential damping. **No match.**

19. Has constant and \(e^{c2 x}\): set \(c0=0,c1=0\). Also has \(v|v|\) term; set \(c7=0\). Then remaining \(c3 v + c4 v^3 + \cos + c8 v e^{c9|v|}\) can match with \(c9=-1\) and phase shift. **Match possible.**

20. Has \(v|v|\) and \(v\log(\cdot)|v|\); set \(c4=0,c5=0\). Then has \(c0 v + \cos + c7 v e^{c8|v|}\) but no \(v^3\). **No match.**

21. Has constant and \(e^{c2 x}\): set \(c0=0,c1=0\). Has extra \(v x^2\) term: must set \(c3=0\). Then has \(v^3\), \(\cos\), \(v e^{c8|v|}\), and linear \(c9 v\). Choose \(c8=-1\) and phase shift. **Match possible.**

22. Has constant and \(e^{c2 x}\): set \(c0=0,c1=0\). Has \(\log(c5 v+1)\) term; GT has none so set \(c4=0\). Then has \(c3 v^3 + \cos + c8 v e^{c9|v|}\). Missing linear \(v\) unless embedded elsewhere (not). **No match.**

23. Has \(v\), \(\cos\), \(v e^{c8|v|}\) but also \(\sin(c3 v + c4)\) (depends on \(v\)); set its coefficient \(c2=0\). Then still no \(v^3\). **No match.**

24. \(c0 v + c1 v^3 + c2\cos(c3+t) + c4 v^{c5} + c6 v^{c7} e^{c8|v|}\)  
   Need exactly one linear, one cubic, and \(v e^{-|v|}\). Set \(c4=0\) to remove extra power term. Set \(c7=1\), \(c8=-1\) so \(c6 v e^{-|v|}\). Then match coefficients and trig phase. **Match possible.**

25. Has extra \(\sin(c4 v + c5)\) term; set \(c3=0\). Then it’s \(v\), \(\cos\), \(v e^{c7|v|}\) but no \(v^3\). **No match.**

26. Has constant and \(e^{c6 t}\) and \(v|v|\) and rational term; can zero extras, but there is no \(v^3\) and no \(v e^{-|v|}\). **No match.**

27. \(c0 + c1 v + c2 v^3 + c3\cos(c4+t) + c5 v e^{c6|v|}\)  
   Set constant \(c0=0\). Choose \(c6=-1\). Choose trig phase to match sine. Set coefficients to GT. **Match possible.**

28. Similar to 27 with two cubic coefficients; set \(c0=0\), combine cubics to match, set \(c6=-1\), set linear \(c7 v\) to match, trig phase shift. **Match possible.**

29. Similar: set \(c0=0\), combine linear terms \(c1 v + c2 v\), set \(c7\) for cubic, set \(c6=-1\), trig phase shift. **Match possible.**

30. \(c0 v + c1 + c2\cos(c3+t) + c4 v^{c5} + c6 v e^{c7|v|}\)  
   Set \(c1=0\). Need both \(v\) and \(v^3\): can set \(c5=3\) for cubic, but then no separate linear unless \(c0 v\) provides it (yes). Set \(c7=-1\). Trig phase shift. **Match possible.**

31. Has extra \(v|v|\); set \(c5=0\). Also has constant; set \(c0=0\). Then matches 27 form. **Match possible.**

32. Has rational \(v/(c6+|v|)\) term; set \(c5=0\). Also has constant; set \(c0=0\). Then left with \(c1 v + \cos + c7 v e^{c8|v|}\) and no \(v^3\). **No match.**

33. Has constant; set \(c0=0\). Has \(c1 v\) and \(c8 v\) combine to linear. Has \(v^3\). Has \(\cos(c4 t + c5)\): set \(c4=1\) and phase shift. Has \(v e^{c7|v|}\): set \(c7=-1\). **Match possible.**

34. Has constant; set \(c0=0\). Has \(v^{c6}\): set \(c6=3\) and use that as cubic. Has linear \(c1 v\). Has exp term with \(|v|\): set exponent coefficient \(-1\). Trig: set frequency \(c3=1\) and phase shift. **Match possible.**

35. Has constant; set \(c0=0\). Has linear \(c1 v\), cubic \(c5 v^3\), trig with adjustable frequency \(c3\) (set \(=1\) and phase), and exp term (set exponent \(-1\)). **Match possible.**

37-38. Built from \(v|v|\), rational, log terms; no \(v^3\) and no \(v e^{-|v|}\). **No match** for both.

39. All terms divided by \(c3+|v|\) and include \(|v|\) factors; GT has no such denominator. Only way is impossible globally (can’t make denominator constant for all \(v\)). **No match.**

40-41. Include \(v|v|\) and log/exp-in-t; no \(v^3\) and no \(v e^{-|v|}\). **No match.**
